    if (!selectedCategory) return;
    const updateTree = (items) => {
      return items.map((item) => {
        if (item.type === "folder" && item.id === folderId) {
          return { ...item, expanded: !item.expanded };
        }
        if (item.type === "folder") {
          return { ...item, children: updateTree(item.children) };
        }
        return item;
      });
    };
    setTreeData({
      ...treeData,
      [selectedCategory]: updateTree(treeData[selectedCategory])
    });
  };
  const openDocument = (doc) => {
    setSelectedDocument(doc);
    setDocumentTitle(doc.name);
    setCurrentMetadata(doc.metadata);
    setDocumentContent(doc.content || generateSampleContent(doc));
    setShowMetadataPanel(true);
    setCurrentView("editor");
  };

      return items.map((item) => {
        if (item.type === "folder" && item.sector === sector && item.id.startsWith("sector-")) {

        if (item.type === "folder") {
          return { ...item, children: updateTree(item.children) };
        }
        return item;
      });
    };

      ...treeData,
      [selectedCategory]: updateTree(treeData[selectedCategory])
    });
